In [7]:
strEx = " ".join(str(x) for x in ex)
In [8]:
def preprocess(sent):
    sent = nltk.word_tokenize(sent)
    sent = nltk.pos_tag(sent)
    return sent
In [9]:

自訂名詞片語 NP = 組織 ORG + 動詞 VB + 名詞 NN
In [22]:
pattern = 'NP: {<ORG>*<VB>*<NN>}'
cp = nltk.RegexpParser(pattern)
cs = cp.parse(sent)
print(cs)

tree1 = nltk.Tree('NP',['US'])
print(tree1)
tree2 = nltk.Tree('N',['US','immigrate'])

tree3 = nltk.Tree('S',[tree1,tree2])
print(tree3.label())

In [16]:
def get_continuous_chunks(text, label):
    chunked = ne_chunk(pos_tag(word_tokenize(text)))
    prev = None
    continuous_chunk = []
    current_chunk = []

    for subtree in chunked:
        if type(subtree) == Tree and subtree.label() == label:
            current_chunk.append(" ".join([token for token, pos in subtree.leaves()]))
        elif current_chunk:
            named_entity = " ".join(current_chunk)
            if named_entity not in continuous_chunk:
                continuous_chunk.append(named_entity)
                current_chunk = []
        else:
            continue

    return continuous_chunk

get_continuous_chunks(strEx, 'FACILITY')

In [ ]:
查詢Organization，針對一些沒看過的組織名稱做查詢，可以更深入了解移民問題的相關單位或是專有名詞。
例如，EADAP,應該寫為EAD/AP ==> Employment Authorization Document (工作簽證) & Advance Parole permission (允許你出入美國旅遊，但不影響綠卡申請程序)
兩者一起來會稱為"combo card"。
